## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t, which is the central problem in population dynamics. Classical models range from simple exponential/logistic growth to more complex formulations with Allee effects, density dependence, and time-varying parameters.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (exponential growth, density-independent)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 * P) (logarithmic density dependence)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P + c1) * (1 + c2 * P) (growth negative below critical threshold)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P**c2) (generalized density dependence)
- Beverton-Holt type: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (rational density dependence)
- Logistic with time-varying rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * t) (time-modulated logistic)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (periodic environmental forcing)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P**c2) (flexible inflection point)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (cubic population dynamics)
- Exponential decay rate: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (time-dependent intrinsic rate)
- Von Bertalanffy type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 + c2 * P (allometric growth vs. mortality)
- Delayed density dependence proxy: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * P) + c2 * t * P (time as proxy for lagged effects)
- Hassell-type: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P)**c2 (generalized contest/scramble competition)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P â†’ fundamental mass-action principle: growth rate scales with number of reproducing individuals
- Quadratic term PÂ² with negative coefficient â†’ intraspecific competition or density-dependent mortality
- Cubic term PÂ³ â†’ Allee effect or higher-order density interactions creating multiple equilibria
- Product P*log(P) â†’ Gompertz-type dynamics where per-capita rate decreases logarithmically with density
- Rational form P/(1+cP) â†’ resource competition where growth saturates due to finite resource availability
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) multiplying growth terms â†’ seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
- Fractional powers of P (P^c with 0<c<1) â†’ allometric scaling of metabolic/growth processes
- Multiple roots in dP/dt as function of P â†’ multiple equilibria indicating bistability or regime shifts
- Exponential time factor exp(c*t) â†’ environmental degradation or improvement changing intrinsic growth rate over time
- Ratio structure PÂ²/(1+cPÂ²) â†’ cooperative behavior or mate-finding Allee effect at low densities
